## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x4B00 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x4B01 [0x20] SET_CLI_EVENT_UC_FLAG: Lock player control
  2: 0x4B03 [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Disable user control
  3: 0x4B05 [0x5D] SET_MUSIC_VOLUME(volume=0*, fade_time=180*)
```
